    researcher_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    expertise VARCHAR(255),
    email VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE experiments (
    experiment_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    experiment_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    project_id UUID REFERENCES research_projects(project_id),
    researcher_id UUID REFERENCES researchers(researcher_id),
    start_date TIMESTAMP,
    end_date TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE research_projects (
    project_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    project_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    project_description TEXT,
    start_date DATE,
    end_date DATE
);</t><s>SHOW CREATE TABLE researchers</s>

CREATE TABLE Experiment (experiment_id INT PRIMARY KEY, gene_id INT NOT NULL, protein_id INT NOT NULL, result VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, FOREIGN KEY (gene_id) REFERENCES Gene(gene_id), FOREIGN KEY (protein_id) REFERENCES Protein(protein_id))</t><s>SHOW TABLES</s>
